    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/696042-ls-there-two-different-versions-of-this">ls there two different versions of this story?</a>
</div>
<div class='communityQAFooter questionFooter'>
<ul class='questionFooterActions'>
<li class='footerItem like'>
<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_696042'><a id="like_count_community_question_696042" rel="nofollow" href="/rating/voters/696042?resource_type=CommunityQuestion"><span class="likesCount">1 like</span></a>&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;<a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F18089551-tall-tatted-and-tempting">like</a></span>

<li class='footerItem communityQuestionTimestamp'>
<a href="/questions/696042-ls-there-two-different-versions-of-this">4 years ago</a>
</li>
<li class='footerItem communityQuestionPermalink'>

<div class='allCommunityAnswers'>
<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/28854800-ellen"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1392836385i/28854800._UX100_CR0,11,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/28854800-ellen">Ellen</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">yes-<br/> ­Dear Readers,­I found myself in a little bit of a quandary as I wrote this book. If you’ve read any of my books before, you know that my writing<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">yes-<br /> ­Dear Readers,­I found myself in a little bit of a quandary as I wrote this book. If you’ve read any of my books before, you know that my writing tends to run toward the hot end of thermometer. I write heat because it’s also what I like to read. However, when I was writing this book, my eighteen-­year-­old son was intrigued by the premise, and he asked if he could read some pages early on. As I wrote more and more, he asked for more pages, and finally I got to the point where he could no longer feel comfortable reading it. He asked me for a version “just for him.­” He’s not a prude by any means, but he was more comfortable with a “sexy-­lite” version of the book. My mother is also someone who skips the sex scenes, and she was intrigued when I told her about this special version. Since it was already written, I have included both versions in this compilation. The first version is a hot read, not meant for anyone under the age of eighteen and not meant for those who don’t enjoy explicit sex scenes. The second version is my son’s version. By no means is it meant for anyone under the age of eighteen, since it has adult content, adult language, and adult situations. But it’s sexy-­lite. I hope you like your choice of story and appreciate that the choice of which one to read is yours!­Best regards,­Tammy<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>
</div>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">The H is actually deaf from a childhood fever and chose to be mute because of bullies... But the h doesn't know sign language and has dyslexia, so she<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">The H is actually deaf from a childhood fever and chose to be mute because of bullies... But the h doesn't know sign language and has dyslexia, so she can't easily read notes that he would normally use to communicate to none signers. <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

<div id="review_3571045275" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3571045275" />
    <a title="Anovelqueen " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13460432-anovelqueen"><img alt="Anovelqueen " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1504643001p2/13460432.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3571045275?book_show_action=true">Sep 28, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anovelqueen " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anovelqueen " href="/user/show/13460432-anovelqueen">Anovelqueen </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13460432-anovelqueen?shelf=insta-love">insta-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13460432-anovelqueen?shelf=bad-boys-tattoos">bad-boys-tattoos</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13460432-anovelqueen?shelf=college-romance">college-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3571045275" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16139204869864283127">***3.5 STARS***<br/><br/>This was a very difficult book to rate. Although I found it had a lot of fluff I couldn’t stop reading it and had to see how it ended. So it did keep my attention.<br/><br/>Kit comes into the tattoo shop where Logan works as an artist wanting a tattoo she designed herself. She winds up hitting Logan in the nose when he becomes overly familiar with her. Later he finds her again while she is busking at a subway station. He follows her and realizes she is homeless so he feeds her and takes her</span>
  <span id="freeText16139204869864283127" style="display:none">***3.5 STARS***<br /><br />This was a very difficult book to rate. Although I found it had a lot of fluff I couldn’t stop reading it and had to see how it ended. So it did keep my attention.<br /><br />Kit comes into the tattoo shop where Logan works as an artist wanting a tattoo she designed herself. She winds up hitting Logan in the nose when he becomes overly familiar with her. Later he finds her again while she is busking at a subway station. He follows her and realizes she is homeless so he feeds her and takes her back to his apartment where he lives with his four brothers.<br /><br />I found Logan adorable. He is a huge hunk of a guy that is intelligent, an excellent artist and happens to be deaf. Kit is on the run from a secretive life and it takes the majority of the book before she reveals her true identity. It was a little anticlimactic in my opinion. But like I said before I couldn’t stop reading. So what does that say? The book kept my interest, but if you are looking for a deep and eternal romance here you will not find it. First they are very young. She is 19 and he is 21. Secondly, they fall into lust instantly. <br /><br />It was a quick and interesting read. Not the best but not the worst either. I will definitely read the next book as this one ends on a cliffhanger. I did love the relationship Logan had with his brothers. It was realistic and loving. </span>
  <a data-text-id="16139204869864283127" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_679810302" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/679810302" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/679810302?book_show_action=true">Jul 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Christy by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/6744426-anna">Anna</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer679810302" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8943755501989490951"><b>4 Stars!</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/4b3e44ae-4427-4f4c-aae7-d583337cc857_zps7a8fb37f.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430929i/864336.jpg' alt=' photo 4b3e44ae-4427-4f4c-aae7-d583337cc857_zps7a8fb37f.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><i>Tall, Tatted and Tempting</i> is the perfect title for this book- it describes Logan just right! <br/><br/><b><u>Logan: </u><br/>No one really talks to me since I can’t hear. I haven’t said a word since I was thirteen years old.</b><br/><br/>Logan lives with his four brothers. He is a tattoo artist. He is a bit of a man slut. And he is also deaf.<br/><br/><b><u>Emily:</u> <br/>Home is a relative term. Home is wherever I find to sleep that night.</b><br/><br/>  Emily goes by Kit. She spends her days playing guitar by the subway of NYC. She is a long way from home. </span>
  <span id="freeText8943755501989490951" style="display:none"><b>4 Stars!</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/4b3e44ae-4427-4f4c-aae7-d583337cc857_zps7a8fb37f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430929i/864336.jpg" alt=" photo 4b3e44ae-4427-4f4c-aae7-d583337cc857_zps7a8fb37f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Tall, Tatted and Tempting</i> is the perfect title for this book- it describes Logan just right! <br><br><b><u>Logan: </u><br>No one really talks to me since I can’t hear. I haven’t said a word since I was thirteen years old.</b><br><br>Logan lives with his four brothers. He is a tattoo artist. He is a bit of a man slut. And he is also deaf.<br><br><b><u>Emily:</u> <br>Home is a relative term. Home is wherever I find to sleep that night.</b><br><br>  Emily goes by Kit. She spends her days playing guitar by the subway of NYC. She is a long way from home. She comes from a whole different world than the one she is living in now. She is homeless- but it’s a choice she made. <br><br>If I told you Emily and Logan hit it off right away, I would be lying. It takes some time, but Logan is persistent. There is something about this girl who wanders into the tattoo parlor. They start out with an uneasy friendship. Their communication is difficult at first. Logan can’t hear, and Emily has a condition that makes it hard for her to read. They resort to lip reading and Logan, for the first time in years, talks. But only to her. He finds Emily is different than any girl he’s ever met. He wants her, but she is still hiding so much of herself. Until she can trust him and let him in, he won’t take it past friendship. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I want you to trust me. And you don’t. Not yet. But you might one day.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>She is developing feelings for him...<br><i>
  <blockquote>“I think I’m in like.”</blockquote>
</i><br>He has some strong feelings for her...<br><i>
  <blockquote>“I want you more than I want air.”</blockquote>
</i><br>But Emily still doesn’t feel like she can open up to him. It’s not that she doesn’t want to, she just can’t. She has her reasons. She won’t even tell him her name, which doesn’t sit well with him. Before he can be with her completely, he has to know her. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“If I ever get to fucking be inside you, I want to know what to call you. I want to at least know your name. Because when that happens, you’re going to fucking own me. Do you understand? You’re going to own me.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Emily is getting there. She is falling hard for Logan, she fits with his family. For the first time in months, she feels safe. Happy. Loved. But something will happen that will change everything. She has a choice to make, and it’s not an easy one... <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/3659e5e8-dbb4-44cf-9fcd-9f6c0392af7a_zpscd14a943.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430929i/864337.jpg" alt=" photo 3659e5e8-dbb4-44cf-9fcd-9f6c0392af7a_zpscd14a943.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>I want all of her. I want her past, her present, and her future.</b><br><br> I just love a good story about a reformed man-whore! When they find that one person who changes their ways. Logan was so adorable- and funny! He has never really had a ‘girlfriend’ but his description of one just cracked me up! <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I want you to be my girlfriend.” <br><br>“What does that mean?”<br><br> “I’m not sure. but I think it’s the same as being my friend, but I get to make you come.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>There is just no way you won’t fall for Logan. He appears to be a ‘bad boy’ but once you get to know him, he has the biggest heart. He was just so sweet and swoony! <br><i>
  <blockquote>She laughs. I wish I could hear it, because its probably the most beautiful sound in the world. It's not often I wish I could hear, because I can do almost anything I want. But right now, I wish I could hear the sound of her laughter.</blockquote>
</i><br>Emily was a wonderful heroine. She had obstacles to overcome, just like Logan. She was strong and resilient. I do wish she could have trusted Logan more with her secrets, but I understood why she didn’t. She was willing to sacrifice everything she had worked for, give it all up for the person she loved. So many times her her actions show how much character she has. <br><br>I family dynamic in this book was great. Even though Logan had no parents to speak of, his brothers were a tight unit. I especially had a soft spot for Matt and Paul. I can’t wait to read more about the Reed brothers in the following books. <br><br>This book captured my attention right away. The characters were endearing, the story was fast paced, interesting and refreshing. Lets just say a few pages in and I was hooked. By the time I hit the ending, I was disappointed it was over so quickly! The last few chapters had me on the edge of my seat... I was so worried with how it was going to end- but the ending wasn’t as cliffy as I thought it would be, and thankfully, the author has posted the first chapter of the second book (see link at bottom of review). I would recommend reading that as soon as you finish this book. It will make your heart happy! <br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://tammyfalkner.wordpress.com/2013/07/10/chapter-one-unedited-of-smart-sexy-and-secretive/">http://tammyfalkner.wordpress.com/201...</a><br><br>Big thanks to my bestie, Anna, for recommending this one to me and talking me through the last 15% or so when I was a little on edge ;)) Love ya! xoxo!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="8943755501989490951" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1288729254" />
    <a title="Melissa (Ever So Mela)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28640648-melissa-ever-so-mela"><img alt="Melissa (Ever So Mela)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487543962p2/28640648.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1288729254?book_show_action=true">May 24, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melissa (Ever So Mela)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melissa (Ever So Mela)" href="/user/show/28640648-melissa-ever-so-mela">Melissa (Ever So Mela)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28640648-melissa-ever-so-mela?shelf=na-romance">na-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28640648-melissa-ever-so-mela?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28640648-melissa-ever-so-mela?shelf=women-are-not-this-stupid">women-are-not-this-stupid</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1288729254" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9451596770349284473"><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>I just read the most epic love story!</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br/>I mean, there is love and then there's <i>Kit and Logan love</i>. But let me not get ahead of myself. Let's start at the beginning. <br/><br/>So on <b>Monday</b> we're introduced to Kit. She's broke and homeless but a fighter nonetheless, busking at the train station. I mean if that doesn't scream strong and independent, I don't know what does. And <i>guess what</i>? <b>She has a secret!</b> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420118374ra/13175394.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Bet you did not see <i>that</i> coming!<br/><br/>And then things get good and she meets our tall, tatted, and t</span>
  <span id="freeText9451596770349284473" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>I just read the most epic love story!</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>I mean, there is love and then there's <i>Kit and Logan love</i>. But let me not get ahead of myself. Let's start at the beginning. <br><br>So on <b>Monday</b> we're introduced to Kit. She's broke and homeless but a fighter nonetheless, busking at the train station. I mean if that doesn't scream strong and independent, I don't know what does. And <i>guess what</i>? <b>She has a secret!</b> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420118374ra/13175394.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Bet you did not see <i>that</i> coming!<br><br>And then things get good and she meets our tall, tatted, and tempting loverboy, Logan. He's so unique he's deaf. Can't get anymore original than that people!<b>duh!</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1414337160ra/11641648.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>On <b>Wednesday</b> they meet again and she ends up sleeping at his house. We're blessed with the seeds of their growing love when...<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"She closes the door behind me and I <u>hear</u> the thumb lock on the door click. She just locked me out of my own room."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>True love?? True love makes the deaf hear!!<br>And by <b>Friday</b> she's falling...<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>And I’m afraid I’m a little bit in love with Logan.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422217ra/839745.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>By <b>Saturday</b> they're confessing.<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I think I might be falling in love with you,” he says softly. My breath catches. “Yeah, me too,” I say.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <br>And two weeks after that he's<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"I want all of her. I want her past, her present and her future. I want to ask her to marry me."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435078802ra/15299494.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>By this time she's also a full blown pro at sign language. I mean girl understands everything and can perfectly sign whole conversations. You know, something that takes people months and months to learn, she learns it in <b>two.weeks.</b> I'm telling you, it's this true love. It makes miracles happen. <br><br>So now you understand you can say it right along with me...<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>I just read the most epic love story!</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434991496ra/15288413.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

<div id="review_684281581" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/684281581" />
    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/684281581?book_show_action=true">Aug 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">EVERYONE </span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to • Lisa • by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/6744426-anna">Anna</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer684281581" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1533416466519954789"><b>5 'JUST MY CUPPA' STARS.</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"I love you New York. Never doubt it."</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431561i/866059._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431561i/866060._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Three words to start my review <b>READ.THIS.BOOK</b>,When my friend texted me telling me about this story, I thought why not? I'll give this book a try, what I didn't expect was to fall so in love with two characters and this deliciously written novel. 'Tall, tatted and tempting' is so much more than its title suggests. It is full of heart and soul and is written to heart warmingly wonderful proportions. This story has completely capture</span>
  <span id="freeText1533416466519954789" style="display:none"><b>5 'JUST MY CUPPA' STARS.</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"I love you New York. Never doubt it."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431561i/866059._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431561i/866060._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Three words to start my review <b>READ.THIS.BOOK</b>,When my friend texted me telling me about this story, I thought why not? I'll give this book a try, what I didn't expect was to fall so in love with two characters and this deliciously written novel. 'Tall, tatted and tempting' is so much more than its title suggests. It is full of heart and soul and is written to heart warmingly wonderful proportions. This story has completely captured my heart and attention and I will gladly crown it with the title 'one of my favourite stories of 2013'.<br><br><b>What's it all about?</b><br>Emily Madison isn't a young woman who feels hope, she's a lost soul desperate to not feel, anxious to keep her secrets, and to live a life unanswerable to no one, living her life as she pleases. With a life of homelessness and surviving this life by busking Emily 'Kit' Madison believes living a life in isolation is the only way to live, that is until a curly blonde haired stranger comes into her life, Logan Reed is a tattooed, deaf and drop dead loveable man who has never been interested in holding on to any kind of serious relationship but when these two lives collide they both find themselves questioning their respective lifestyles. Can love overcome secrets, heartache and difficulties? 'Tall, tattooed and tempted' takes us through this duo's story towards a hopefully happily love forever.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431561i/866061._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What did I love?</b><br>For a short book, this story had depth and emotion by the chapterful I was so wrapped up in the characters and plot that I was surprised when I got to the end. 'Tall, tatted and tempting' is full to the brim with secrets and surprises and it is so refreshingly different that I'm already reaching to find more by this author. I love both the characters Emily is brave, courageous and sweet, I love that she was making her own way in life. Emily is both confident and vulnerable the perfect 'other half' for the books hero, Logan I loved his strength in the face of his deafness, the author brought the connection between these loveable characters to life and the sexual Chemistry was off the scales I thought I might have spontaneously combusted on more than one occasion as the story developed. This book was writing perfection I loved every moment right from the first page. I do not have one negative thing to say about this sweet and touching story.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431561i/866062._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Final thoughts ...</b><br>Don't miss out on this gorgeous, sweet and moving story. Although it is relatively short it packs more than a romantic punch and I'm convinced like me once you have read it you will be ready for more in the series. Heartbreaking and romantic in equal measure I know I have found a series I'll hold close to my book heart. Go grab it readers.<br><br>*As a word of caution, although this book does not have a cliffhanger it leaves the story wide open for book two here's a link to click straight after finishing this story*<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://tammyfalkner.wordpress.com/2013/07/10/chapter-one-unedited-of-smart-sexy-and-secretive/">http://tammyfalkner.wordpress.com/201...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="1533416466519954789" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer18428125480710139588"><strong>Tall, Tatted, Tempting and the sexiest deaf mute I’ve ever read about!</strong><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1564552204ra/27915489.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I really enjoyed this romance between Logan Reed, a Tattoo artist and deaf mute who is usually a hit it and quit it kind of guy with the ladies and Kit, a homeless girl who plays guitar in the subway station for dollars and change. The romance is downright steamy even though Logan is determined not to go all the way until Kit trusts him enough to tell him her real name.<br/><br/>The character development in this story is awesome. It is </span>
  <span id="freeText18428125480710139588" style="display:none"><strong>Tall, Tatted, Tempting and the sexiest deaf mute I’ve ever read about!</strong><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1564552204ra/27915489.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I really enjoyed this romance between Logan Reed, a Tattoo artist and deaf mute who is usually a hit it and quit it kind of guy with the ladies and Kit, a homeless girl who plays guitar in the subway station for dollars and change. The romance is downright steamy even though Logan is determined not to go all the way until Kit trusts him enough to tell him her real name.<br><br>The character development in this story is awesome. It is the first book in the Reed brothers series and Kit stays with the brothers so they are all introduced in this book. We find out more about some of them than others, but definitely enough to pull at the old heartstrings. <br><br>I am already completely enamored with Logan, Paul and especially Matt. Kit (a.k.a. Emily) also has developed close relationships with the brothers, especially Matt, who has cancer, and Paul, the oldest who has a daughter. There are also twins that are still in high school which we need to know more about, so the series should be great. <br><br>This particular book ends on a cliffhanger so I am going to have to get the next book to find out what happens between Logan and His girl. It is worth it though, just the right mix between romance, steam and drama.<br><br>I voluntarily read &amp; reviewed an advanced copy of this book. <div id="review_793438799" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/793438799" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/793438799?book_show_action=true">Dec 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer793438799" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4913833327156320589"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387646317i/7641952._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>First, here's my casting for Logan ;) </i><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387561520i/7620577._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387586332ra/7625309.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ** <b>4.5 stars!! </b><br/><br/><b> OMG!!! Guys, this book was awesome!!<br/><br/><em>Tall, Tatted, and Tempting</em> was a sweet, sexy and very moving story with a wonderful balance of humor, steam, and also heartfelt, emotional depth! I loved it! </b><br/><br/>A friend of mine actually recommended it to me and after reading this section of the blurb, I knew this was one I had to check out....<br/><br/><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Logan Reed is tall, tatted and tempting. Kit’s a woman with a mean right hook and a</em></blockquote></b></span>
  <span id="freeText4913833327156320589" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387646317i/7641952._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>First, here's my casting for Logan ;) </i><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387561520i/7620577._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387586332ra/7625309.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ** <b>4.5 stars!! </b><br><br><b> OMG!!! Guys, this book was awesome!!<br><br><em>Tall, Tatted, and Tempting</em> was a sweet, sexy and very moving story with a wonderful balance of humor, steam, and also heartfelt, emotional depth! I loved it! </b><br><br>A friend of mine actually recommended it to me and after reading this section of the blurb, I knew this was one I had to check out....<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Logan Reed is tall, tatted and tempting. Kit’s a woman with a mean right hook and a secret. Kit wants a tattoo, but Logan sees more than she intends to share in the drawing of the tat she wants. He sees her in ways no one ever has. Logan’s not disabled; but he hasn’t spoken in eight years. He hasn’t needed to. Until he meets Kit."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>As it hinted there, we learn in the first scene that the hero of the story, Logan, was tall and gorgeous but also deaf and hadn't spoken to anyone since he was 13. He ran a tattoo parlor with his four brothers which was where he was working in the opening scene. And then a girl walked in asking for a very specific tattoo and he felt drawn to her in a way he'd never once felt before....<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Most people would see the beauty of that drawing. But I see pain. I see things she probably wouldn't want anyone to see."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Ok, at this point, even though I was smiling, I totally thought I could tell where the story was going... But then, about one minute into their interaction, this girl punched him in the face and walked out the door!!!!<br><br>OMG!! That was it. With that scene, I was hooked me! The opening chapter alone had made me smile, surprised me, and intrigued me to want to know more about the characters.<br><br>So...  Logan wasn't able to stop thinking about her and finally tracked her down to the last place on earth he thought to find her -- homeless and playing music on the streets to make enough money to get by.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Does she own a coat? I wish I'd given her mine. I follow her. I can't help it. I need to see where she's going, or I won't be able to find her again. Not to mention that her being alone in the night in the city scares the shit out of me."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>And he insisted she comes home with him to stay with him and his brothers. While she was grateful for the place to stay, she was not the kind of girl to just accept charity and her past had taught her not to trust anyone so she kept a lot back from Logan and felt unable to trust him with her secrets. But luckily, he understood and was falling for her hard enough to make her worth the wait..... :)<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I want to lick you all over and make you cry out my name and swear you see God, I want you to trust me. And you don't. Not Yet. But you might one day."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>I'll let you discover the rest of the story for yourselves from this point on because it's more fun that way so all I'll say is that I loved the whole overall storyline and was totally wrapped up in it.<br><br>The writing was so addictive!! I literally started the book and even though it was a full length novel, I was at 12% before I knew it -- I didn't even realize how many pages I'd been quickly flipping!<br><br>Now, given that Logan lived with his four brothers, there was a helluva lot of testosterone and general male awesome going around. Their parents weren't in their lives, so they'd developed a very tight-knit bond -- they always had each other's backs and each one of them would have been willing to give up anything for the other. I was in Alpha male heaven!! Plus, they were downright hilarious :D<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I go get another beer, and Paul glares at me like the time I let the toilet lid fall on his dick when he was seven and I was four."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>I loved each one of them and also loved they all had their own story to tell. I loved Paul &amp; Hayley, I laughed over the twins, my heart bled for Matt, and it melted for Logan.<br><br>Logan was just a dream. What an absolute sweetheart of a guy!!! He tugged my heart strings and had me fanning myself over and over and over again! He was the kind of guy that is impossible not to fall for. But what stood out most to me about him though was his personality. There's something about the tattooed ex-manwhore who falls for this <em>one</em> special girl that makes me swoon. And Logan just had the biggest heart and had a very distinctive, memorable quality to him. I loved that I could <em>feel</em> how strongly he was falling for her and I loved that he made my heart flutter with almost anything he did.<br><br>And the heroine was also totally awesome as well -- what a badass chick!! It was so nice to see a female character who was able to defend herself, didn't blink once about punching a guy twice her size in the nose and just who didn't take any shit from anyone. But she was also incredibly kind, loving, and caring and over the course of this story proved how she was willing to sacrifice anything for the people she loved.<br><br>It was so cute and endearing watching Logan and Kit get to know each other and I especially loved the way sign language was incorporated into the story. I also really appreciated that he didn't let anything stupid get between them and was willing to be patient while he waited for her to learn to trust him. But... that didn't mean he didn't want more ;)<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I want to be your friend," I say.</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em>"I want you to be my girlfriend."</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em>"What does that mean?" ….</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em>He looks confused. "I'm not sure. But I think it's the same as being my friend, but I get to make you come."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>I also absolutely adored all the interactions and connections between the characters. The way the author described all the little details, actions and thoughts brought the story to life so vividly in my mind. I laughed with them, swooned and even cried! Honestly, even though the writing style &amp; story was completely different, it almost reminded me in a way of Kristen Ashley's books just in the sense of how strongly I was drawn into every little interactive detail. It was definitely one of the highlights of the book for me.<br><br>Also, the book took me completely by surprise with a <em>very</em> emotional turn of the story in the second half that actually made me wipe tears away while I was reading. The emotions hit me strongly and brought an added depth to the overall story, really rounding everything out.<br><br>Overall, I'd say this was a sweet, well written, wonderful story that just drew me right in and kept me connected. It had great characters and plenty of steam and fun, but was also balanced out by a lot of heartfelt emotion. It was a full length novel, but also a quick, easy read. I loved it the whole way through and would totally recommend you check it out!!<br><br>This is the first of a series called "The Reed Brothers". The second book is focused on the same couple as this book so the ending does leave you immediately wanting to read the next book. Luckily, that book has already been released, and also, even if you don't have time to read both books immediately, there is a bonus "first chapter" from the second book at the end of this one that will answer the one major question that you were left with so really, I'd call it a very "safe-to-start" book :)<br><br><strong>Rating: 4.5 stars</strong><br><br><i> ** NOTE: Both Books #1 + 2 focus on the same couple. Even though in the blurbs, the heroine's name is different, they are the same girl. She just doesn't tell him her real name til the end of the first one even though the reader knows it. So, Kit + Emily are the same person. I just don't want you to worry that the hero is with two different girls in a row because that's not the case ;) </i><br><br>****************************<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>

  <span id="freeText9891002444658250154" style="display:none">This was a sweet, inspiring and heartfelt story. It was about overcoming obstacles and disproving stereotypes. Kit and Logan forged their own way, falling in love in the process. <br /><br />Kit would rather live on the streets than to return home to the fate that awaits her. When her path crosses with Logan, he quickly realizes that she isn't like the hordes of other girls that fill his nights with meaningless sexual encounters. He is determined to get to know this mysterious runaway. <br /><br />When he offers her a place to stay for the night, Kit doesn't plan on finding a home and family amongst Logan and his brothers. Logan didn't know that this beautiful girl would tear down the walls he'd built up over the years to protect himself from the pain of rejection. Neither of them could have predicted the love that would grow from acceptance.<br /><br />I enjoyed every minute of this story. It was sweet and heartwarming. I only wish I'd read this one sooner.</span>

He doesn’t need. <br/>He is also a bit (okay, a lot) of a man-whore. He’s the deaf guy who is pr</span>
  <span id="freeText1542432671198769220" style="display:none"><b>4,5 “Why this tatted book guys are always so hot?” Stars! </b>	<br><br>Emily (Kit) is far away from home and running from her past. She lives on the streets and tries to take as much as she can from life.<br>Her past, her secrets doesn’t allow her to get close to anything or anyone but all that changes in the moment that she decides to make a tattoo. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386637548i/7410980.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Logan is deaf since he was thirteen years and doesn’t talk to anybody. He doesn’t need. <br>He is also a bit (okay, a lot) of a man-whore. He’s the deaf guy who is pretty good in bed and all the girls want to try because they don’t have to worry pretending: He doesn’t listen or talk anyway. He’s also good with that, doesn’t want commitment for that matter. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383157952ra/6419764.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When Emily goes to him to make her a tattoo he thinks that she is just another one wanting him, and acts that way. Well, he soon finds out that she is not interested in him, in a pretty hurtful way. Literally. <br>And when their paths eventually bring them together and they start to develop a friendship (that pretty soon turns into something more), they both have to deal with what it will change in their lives. And they both will find out that no matter how good secrets are hidden… they will always find a way to be revealed. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386637548ra/7410981.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sometimes when you start a book you expect him to be light, easy and fast to read. Just another book in the many ones you read. Sometimes they are just that: one more book. And sometimes they turn into a so much more emotional and amazing ride that you were expecting. <br>That was happened with this book, I was expecting light and got a heavy emotional book, beautiful written and way more gut wrenching that what I thought when I picked it. <br>And I loved it. <br>The characters are great and the story is sweet and amazing. Can’t wait to read the next one in the series! ;)</span>
  <a data-text-id="1542432671198769220" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Logan is the tattoo artist for this project. The sparks fly between them especially when Emily ends up punching him in the nose and breaking it.<br/><br/><b>Together</b> they each share a</span>
  <span id="freeText13970705222313247645" style="display:none">***3.75 stars***<br><br><u>Tall, Tatted and Tempting</u> has been getting rave reviews because of<b> one unique character- Logan. </b> Logan's deaf and has been living in a silent world since he was 13.<b> Emily (‘Kit’)</b> is a homeless girl with a secret past that she's hiding from. <br><br>Emily arrives at a tattoo parlor requesting a tattoo of one her designs. Logan is the tattoo artist for this project. The sparks fly between them especially when Emily ends up punching him in the nose and breaking it.<br><br><b>Together</b> they each share a secret that no one else no knows about <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[- Logan can speak and only does so to Emily. He stopped speaking when other kids made fun of him when he was 13 years old. Emily has a learning disability; she is unable to read.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>The dual POVs allows the reader to experience Logan’s world of<i> silence. </i>The reader achieves a sense of the quietness that surrounds the deaf. Emily learns to read non verbal cues so she can communicate with Logan. <br><br><i>Trust is a huge stumbling block in their relationship. </i> Not sharing who she is or her real name stalls their relationship.<blockquote> <i>”Emily Madison.” <br>My name. It’s Emily Madison.”</i>

To read an excerpt from book two <a>click here.</a><br><br>On a side note: this book had a <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13038680.Poughkeepsie__Poughkeepsie___1_" title="Poughkeepsie (Poughkeepsie, #1) by Debra Anastasia" rel="nofollow noopener">Poughkeepsie</a> vibe. <div id="review_703402292" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/703402292" />
    <a title="Karla" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3024056-karla"><img alt="Karla" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1324910771p2/3024056.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/703402292?book_show_action=true">Aug 25, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karla" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karla" href="/user/show/3024056-karla">Karla</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=2-points-of-view">2-points-of-view</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=exceeded-my-expectations">exceeded-my-expectations</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=strong-willed-heroine">strong-willed-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=passionate">passionate</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=overcoming-tragedy">overcoming-tragedy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=terrific-dialogue">terrific-dialogue</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=set-up-for-series">set-up-for-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=wonderful-secondary-characters">wonderful-secondary-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=second-chance">second-chance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=scrumptious-hero">scrumptious-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer703402292" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11178654100856434664"><br/><b> 4 Pleasantly Surprised Stars! </b> <br/><br/>Told from alternating points of view, Logan and Emily's, this book had an interesting plot. Logan and Emily are each dealing with their own personal struggles, and although a little over the top at times, as far as the storyline goes, it’s not too angsty or overly dramatic. <br/><br/>Emily and Logan form a connection early on and the chemistry between them is quite believable, but what I really loved is the relationship she forms with all his brothers and that the brothers </span>
  <span id="freeText11178654100856434664" style="display:none"><br /><b> 4 Pleasantly Surprised Stars! </b> <br /><br />Told from alternating points of view, Logan and Emily's, this book had an interesting plot. Logan and Emily are each dealing with their own personal struggles, and although a little over the top at times, as far as the storyline goes, it’s not too angsty or overly dramatic. <br /><br />Emily and Logan form a connection early on and the chemistry between them is quite believable, but what I really loved is the relationship she forms with all his brothers and that the brothers have with each other. We could have used more on what brought them to the place they were at, but there was enough information for the reader to piece together their past. <br /><br />Brian from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8135807.Rock_Me__Ross_Siblings___2_" title="Rock Me (Ross Siblings, #2) by Cherrie Lynn" rel="nofollow noopener">Rock Me</a> is one of my all-time favorite pierced, tattooed heroes, but Logan gives him a run for the money. He will satiate readers who are thirsting for the inked, pierced (in all the right places!!) bad boy, who’s tough on the outside, but soft on the inside. Logan's all about his family…his brothers, which I loved, and once he sets his sights on Emily, he’s persistent, but not pushy, in making her his. Hard to explain, but you’ll see. My goodness the boy’s got skills…he will curl your toes!!! <br /><br />I know some readers were not happy with the ending, but I felt it was fitting and satisfying. I can walk away from this book feeling content or choose to continue this series or not. My hope is that Emily and Logan’s story will a sub-plot in the next book and not the main focal point. If the author features another brother, I’m in…as far as I’m concerned Emily and Logan’s story has been told from a relationship standpoint. I wouldn’t mind hearing where they are at and where they are headed, after all this is Logan’s family and he is an everyday presence in their lives. The author just needs to propel them forward, not inject anymore drama into their lives, and leave the drama and angst for another brother…hopefully Paul. If she does that, then this series will set itself apart from the cliffhanger trilogies, or quadlogies…pentlogies...okay so now I’m making up words, you get the picture…that seem to be plaguing the New Adult genre. <br /><br />Despite a few issues; some moments in the book were not quite believable and maybe a little far-fetched, some eye-rolling on my part, but then again we are talking New Adult; I was still captivated from beginning to end. It was sweet, sexy, steamy, and fun. I enjoyed the brothers and the family element; it rounded out the book nicely, the author did a great job on this aspect. Paul, Matt, Pete and Sam all have a story to tell, and as I said, my hope is that the author will feature each and every one of them...would make sense since the series is called <i>The Reed Brothers</i>, and leave the other characters in the background!<br /><br /><i>*Thanks to Lisa P and her review for the heads up on this one!*</i><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11178654100856434664" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=must-read">must-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer685509455" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18329841562709725493"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431733i/866550._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I’m so glad I finally read Tall, Tatted and Tempting! It was everything I needed right now and I did knock my socks off. From painfully heartbreaking to amusing and passionate it blew me away. Why didn’t I read it right after it was released? I still can’t believe I waited so long to do so. I admire Tammy Falkner work and from this point I will be impatiently waiting for her books. I am seriously going to become her fan and stalker number 1. <br/><br/>Anyway, back to the story that swept me away, Tall, Ta</span>
  <span id="freeText18329841562709725493" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431733i/866550._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I’m so glad I finally read Tall, Tatted and Tempting! It was everything I needed right now and I did knock my socks off. From painfully heartbreaking to amusing and passionate it blew me away. Why didn’t I read it right after it was released? I still can’t believe I waited so long to do so. I admire Tammy Falkner work and from this point I will be impatiently waiting for her books. I am seriously going to become her fan and stalker number 1. <br><br>Anyway, back to the story that swept me away, Tall, Tatted and Tempting is fabulous! Great unique concept and phenomenal way of telling the story of two so different people made this book AMAZING. I couldn’t stop reading it till I finished, and after that I started sequel Smart, Sexy and Secretive and finished in mere hours. <br><br>Logan is stunning male character. I fell in love with him on the first page. He’s strong and tatted which makes him incredibly sexy, and what’s more he feels perfectly normal, never finding excuses because he’s deaf. Which makes him even more sexy. Hotness just oozes from him! Well he’s kind of man whore, never caring about women he sleeps with, so when Kit comes to his tattoo parlour to get a tat and punches him so hard his nose bleeds he’s smitten. <br><br>I also adored Kit. I absolutely want her to be my friend (if she really existed). Strong, independent, fierce and talented. The fact that she’s on the run and homeless made me want to give her a hug and help her in every way possible. <br><br>What’s more I loved Logan and Kit together. One of the best couples I’ve read about this year. <br><br>Overall, I immenesly enjoyed Tall, Tatted and Tempting. Author has done fantastic job at creating such realistic story, that so easily blends together heartbreak, passion and great sense of humor. <br><br><br><i>More reviews on <a href="http://smokinhotbookblog.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Smokin' Hot Book Blog</a> and my <a href="https://www.facebook.com/smokinhotbookblog?ref=stream&amp;hc_location=stream" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Page</a></i></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/680285614?book_show_action=true">Jul 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="user" itemprop="url" name="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time">*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer680285614" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13612281587574158594">4.5 Stars!<br/><br/>Well call me crazy but that was....<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400443ra/776008.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Seriously LOVED it! I held off on reading it because I was once again afraid of the dreaded cliffhanger ending. But it wasn't that bad...and it most definitely helped that the author posted chapter one of the next book on her website (see link at the bottom of the review)!<br/><br/>I didn't know it was going to be all sweet and sad and stuff. It was a bit sexy too but with a name like Tall, Tatted and Tempting I thought it was going to be all kinds of smutty. T</span>
  <span id="freeText13612281587574158594" style="display:none">4.5 Stars!<br><br>Well call me crazy but that was....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400443ra/776008.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Seriously LOVED it! I held off on reading it because I was once again afraid of the dreaded cliffhanger ending. But it wasn't that bad...and it most definitely helped that the author posted chapter one of the next book on her website (see link at the bottom of the review)!<br><br>I didn't know it was going to be all sweet and sad and stuff. It was a bit sexy too but with a name like Tall, Tatted and Tempting I thought it was going to be all kinds of smutty. There are two versions a sexy and a sexy-lite. I of course read the sexy version.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380430997ra/864596.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>TTaT is the story of Kit/Emily and Logan. The story started a little something like this....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/280647.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Logan is deaf....and he's also <b>Tall, Tatted and Tempting</b>! He hasn't spoken since he was 13 years old. He lives with his three brothers (including one with cancer, Matt) after their parents died. He works with his family at their tattoo parlor. <br><br>Emily is surviving--not living--on the streets. She plays guitar and sings in the subway to try to get by. Emily is dyslexic. She's on the run, by choice. She doesn't have a home. Emily goes by Kit. <br><br>She meets Logan while trying to get a tattoo. He stares at her boobs, she punches him in the face. He later finds her in the subway singing and so their story begins. Logan and Emily are attracted to each other. Emily is hesitant to open up to Matt because of who her family is. Logan refuses to give himself to Emily until she can trust him completely. <br><br>When Matt's cancer takes a turn for the worse, Emily selflessly gives up her life on the run and returns to the only place she has called home. The End! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421636ra/837800.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>No really, that's how it ended. What's going to happen to Emily and Logan??? Is Matt okay?? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425119ra/848086.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But then I read the first chapter of the next book....<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://tammyfalkner.wordpress.com/2013/07/10/chapter-one-unedited-of-smart-sexy-and-secretive/">http://tammyfalkner.wordpress.com/201...</a><br><br>And now I feel much better!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380430997ra/864597.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="13612281587574158594" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer680439595" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8627120882851104212"><a href='http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/Book%20Boyfriends%20with%20D/Beautiful.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><i>That's how I would describe this story. It gave me those tingly, warm feelings all over and I absolutely loved every second of it. It reminded me of how Callum & Harper made me feel or The Fledgling where you just knew that these two people were made for one another. And best of all it managed to do this in a very well developed story that was interesting and complex and not one bit of corny!!!</i><br/><br/><i>
  <b> ~Emily~ </b>
</i><br/><br/><a href='http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/Emma4.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><i>The moment she walks into the tattoo shop Logan cannot take his eyes off of her. S</i></span>
  <span id="freeText8627120882851104212" style="display:none"><a href="http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/Book%20Boyfriends%20with%20D/Beautiful.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431020i/864651.jpg" alt=" photo Beautiful.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>That's how I would describe this story. It gave me those tingly, warm feelings all over and I absolutely loved every second of it. It reminded me of how Callum &amp; Harper made me feel or The Fledgling where you just knew that these two people were made for one another. And best of all it managed to do this in a very well developed story that was interesting and complex and not one bit of corny!!!</i><br><br><i>
  <b> ~Emily~ </b>
</i><br><br><a href="http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/Emma4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431020i/864652._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Emma4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>The moment she walks into the tattoo shop Logan cannot take his eyes off of her. She isn't just a pretty face though and when he sees the tattoo that she wants he hopes that this is not the last time he ever sees her. </i><br><br><a href="http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/Emma2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431020i/864653._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo Emma2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i> She's a musician, and she takes to his brothers as quickly as she does him. She can admit her feelings and what she really wants but she is also responsible and understands the reality of her situation. Enough so that she holds back in an effort to attempt to protect the man she is quickly falling for. </i><br><br><a href="http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/Emma3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431020i/864654._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Emma3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i> But when everything begins to fall apart for him she makes the ultimate sacrifice with a heavy heart and no guarantees that she will ever have his love again. </i><br><br><a href="http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/letitgo.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431020i/864655.png" alt=" photo letitgo.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>
  <b> ~Logan~ </b>
</i><br><br><a href="http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/LoganTTT3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431020i/864656._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo LoganTTT3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i> He's tatted, pierced, and deaf. He hasn't spoken for years but when he meets Emily he wants to talk to her and he wants her. Even though he knows that she is hiding something major from him and he knows that she will utterly destroy him, he falls fast and hard and is determined to make her his. </i><br><br><a href="http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/love-quotes-breaking-down-walls.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431020i/864657._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo LoganTTT.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i> His world quickly shifts and begins to crumble and he is not sure what the future holds but he knows that she is his and he doesn't want to let her go. </i><br><br><a href="http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/LoganTTT2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431020i/864658._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo LoganTTT2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>In the end will their love conquer all??? </i><br><br><a href="http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/truelove.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1243103844" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1243103844" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505605297p2/13126896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1243103844?book_show_action=true">Apr 01, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1243103844" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12617729966408235474">Tall, Tatted and Tempting by Tammy Falkner<br/>Release information: Released<br/>Series: The Reed Brothers<br/><br/><br/>Logan Reed is one of the five Reed Brothers, one that lost his ability to hear and hasn’t spoken in eight years. Losing their mother at a young age and having their father walk out, the Reed Brothers had to take care of each other. But Logan’s life is about to be turned upside down when Kit walks into the tattoo shop and leaves after punching him in the face. <br/><br/>Kit is running from something. She’s not a</span>
  <span id="freeText12617729966408235474" style="display:none">Tall, Tatted and Tempting by Tammy Falkner<br />Release information: Released<br />Series: The Reed Brothers<br /><br /><br />Logan Reed is one of the five Reed Brothers, one that lost his ability to hear and hasn’t spoken in eight years. Losing their mother at a young age and having their father walk out, the Reed Brothers had to take care of each other. But Logan’s life is about to be turned upside down when Kit walks into the tattoo shop and leaves after punching him in the face. <br /><br />Kit is running from something. She’s not a girl that belongs on the grimy floor of the subway station strumming her guitar for a few bucks. But that is the life she has now. A life that is about to be so much more once she gives in to Logan.<br /><br />There is this instant spark with these two, not instant-love, but a connection that Logan feels instantly. And although Logan isn’t stingy when it comes to sharing his bed, he needs to really know Kit, to have her trust before he’s willing to give all of himself to her. But Kit is running from something and can’t risk getting pulled back into her old life by letting anyone know her secret. <br /><br />I had read one of the other Reed Brother books prior to this one, so I was a little worried that I wouldn’t get the same impact from starting at book one with some knowledge as to the story, I had nothing to worry about. I loved Logan and his need to protect Kit. The way he gave her what she needed but didn’t make it about it being his choice, he allowed her to accept what he was offering. I loved that he spoke for her. That she was what set him free and how easily he shifted to keep it. <br /><br />I have since picked up the remaining books in this series and can’t wait to get to all of the other brother’s stories and to finally finish Logan &amp; Kit’s story in the second installment. No worries if you found yourself reading these out of order, although the couplings are a given, most of the twists are kept out of the other stories – allowing them to be enjoyed as standalones.<br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12617729966408235474" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_2395029937" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2395029937" />
    <a title="Sara➽ Ink Is My Sword" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword"><img alt="Sara➽ Ink Is My Sword" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603584262p2/28146945.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2395029937?book_show_action=true">May 17, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sara➽ Ink Is My Sword" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sara➽ Ink Is My Sword" href="/user/show/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword">Sara➽ Ink Is My Sword</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2395029937" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12481111748503881801"><b>3 “Quick & Addictive” Stars</b><br/><blockquote>
  <i>“And I felt like maybe, just maybe, we were each locked in our own little worlds and could let each other out.”</i>
</blockquote><br/><b>
  <u>➽FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED:</u>
</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1526831051i/25570785.jpg' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Recently I have been in a huge re-reading mood, besides I am just fascinated by how much my reading taste has changed. The way life experiences shape your tolerance to certain things is incredible. So I have decided to call it <b>Throw Back Sara</b> reviews. If you see that you will know it was something a read some time ago and is mos</span>
  <span id="freeText12481111748503881801" style="display:none"><b>3 “Quick &amp; Addictive” Stars</b><br><blockquote>
  <i>“And I felt like maybe, just maybe, we were each locked in our own little worlds and could let each other out.”</i>
</blockquote><br><b>
  <u>➽FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED:</u>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1526831051i/25570785.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Recently I have been in a huge re-reading mood, besides I am just fascinated by how much my reading taste has changed. The way life experiences shape your tolerance to certain things is incredible. So I have decided to call it <b>Throw Back Sara</b> reviews. If you see that you will know it was something a read some time ago and is mostly about how my taste has changed. <br><br>Okay now into the review:<br><br>Have you ever encountered a couple who is about to get married, they look so in love and just ask “So how long were you dating?”. You were never expecting for them to say “Oh, just about a month ago”. You immediately judge because honestly that so fast, and wonder how long are they gonna last, but boom they end up breaking all expectation and grow old together? YEAH, THAT’S EXACTLY THE COUPLE HERE. <br><br><b>The story was addictive, I couldn’t stop reading</b>. I loved how domestic most of the scenes were, brushing teeth, showering, cleaning, eating, just like normal everyday life. Logan’s big family just made all fuzzy, there is something about a big cast family brothers that I love, especially knowing they all have their own book. The Reed family was so supportive and I appreciated how the author didn't shy away from showing monetary struggles and stuff. And Paul's daughter was the cutest, especially how she was learning sign language for her uncle. Finally, I really enjoyed how our hero didn’t budge in the sex department until she could truly trust him. Oh and I need to highlight one scene in the bathroom around 50% in, for me, it was hella hot. <br><br><b>And there were some things I couldn’t get into</b>. Everything was very instant, not saying exactly insta-love, but the protectiveness and jealousy and just confidence between each other were too quick to develop for my taste. The fact he basically started talking to her instead of his own brother was just weird for me. Also, the way dyslexia was handled, just didn’t work for me. I get she was somehow abused because of it, but there wasn’t enough discussion on it and it feels just very hurtful. Finally not something exclusive from the book but a pet peeve of mine in general that I usually hate is the whole “YOU ARE MINE” business. I will say it was a bit tone down and not as annoying but still not something I am a fan of. <br><br>Quick discussion of the ending: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ It felt so resolved and anticlimactic. Also, the first dialogue of the mom was so weird for me. Extremely fake. is something I have encountered a lot in books when characters are supposed to give a touching speech or something, but it doesn't end up being touching. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>TBS:</b> I can totally understand why I gave it 5 stars the first time I read it. It was winter vacation I was bored and this was free on kindle. One of the first new adult romances I read in English and I totally loved it. Now that I have more experience with the genre and I know what I like and what I don’t, I can see this is not perfect by all means. But it certainly delivers in the entertainment factor. <br><br><b>I recommend this if you are starting with the New Adult genre and if you are on vacations and just want something quick but the grips you.</b><br><br><br><b>Pre-reading thoughts:</b><br>Read this one 3 years ago. Only remember our hero may be deaf and has tattoos.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="12481111748503881801" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
