<div id="review_2970431444" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2970431444" />
    <a title="Syndi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1656405-syndi"><img alt="Syndi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1560317991p2/1656405.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2970431444?book_show_action=true">Sep 15, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Syndi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Syndi" href="/user/show/1656405-syndi">Syndi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2970431444" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer755976174382585076"><i> Free copy of kindle edition is provided through Net galley</i><br/><br/>This book is so sweet. I envy this love story between Emily and Logan. Logan is deaf and Emily is dylexia. At first they have trouble communicating at first. But their relationship quickly turns into friendship and love. <br/><br/>What is lacking in this book is the good editing on the wording. The wording is stiff and forced. It does not flow nicely. <br/><br/>Overall i still do enjoy this book very much.<br/><br/>4 stars</span>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_664898681" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/664898681" />
    <a title="Goddess Of Blah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4234324-goddess-of-blah"><img alt="Goddess Of Blah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1284081517p2/4234324.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/664898681?book_show_action=true">Jul 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Goddess Of Blah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Goddess Of Blah" href="/user/show/4234324-goddess-of-blah">Goddess Of Blah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer664898681" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5001540456296282998">YouTube Book Trailer: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=eFj92c25byc&feature=youtu.be'>https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=eFj92...</a><br/><br/>The title and cover of this book does not do it justice. It's not a fluffy chick lit read as the cover and title might suggest. Nor is it the usual run of the mill NA/YA plot. <br/>*Can be read as a Stand Alone or part of sequels. <br/><br/><b>ROMANCE, EXPLOSIVE CHEMISTRY, SENSUAL</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427080371ra/14173748.gif' width='600' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380339038ra/695884.gif' width='600' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>LOVE, GAINING TRUST, FAMILY</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427079391ra/14173550.gif' width='600' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427079391ra/14173551.gif' width='600' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book is <b>extremely engrossing</b>. You're drawn to all the characters and you're really rooting for the Reed family (5 brothers) to make it. <br/>Practic</span>
  <span id="freeText5001540456296282998" style="display:none">YouTube Book Trailer: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=eFj92c25byc&amp;feature=youtu.be">https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=eFj92...</a><br><br>The title and cover of this book does not do it justice. It's not a fluffy chick lit read as the cover and title might suggest. Nor is it the usual run of the mill NA/YA plot. <br>*Can be read as a Stand Alone or part of sequels. <br><br><b>ROMANCE, EXPLOSIVE CHEMISTRY, SENSUAL</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427080371ra/14173748.gif" width="600" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380339038ra/695884.gif" width="600" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>LOVE, GAINING TRUST, FAMILY</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427079391ra/14173550.gif" width="600" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427079391ra/14173551.gif" width="600" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is <b>extremely engrossing</b>. You're drawn to all the characters and you're really rooting for the Reed family (5 brothers) to make it. <br>Practically orphans - they're <b>NOT despondent and melancholy</b> - in fact this book doesn't have any self pitying moments. It's about <u>
  <b>survival</b>
</u> and making the best out of life. <br><br><b>No cliché "broken" "TORMENTED" HEATHCLIFF types. Only survivors building Dreams</b> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427079726ra/14173675.gif" width="600" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The author weaves into the story allowing her readers to engage with the characters. We're invited to understand our protagonist rather than put up with one dimensional characters. <br>For example, <i>how can you not be moved</i> when you learn that a young boy - after becoming <b>deaf at age 13</b> (<i>due to a fever</i>) - <i>stops talking</i> <b>due to kids bully him in the playground</b> - accusing him of sounding like a frog. This is all related in a deadpan, cursory/ conversational manner. No crying pity-me-i'm-so-sad recollections.<br><br>I admire the author for defying the conventions and introducing REAL LIFE issues - with all it's flaws and beauty. <br><b>A deaf hero, a severely dyslexic heroine and a brother fighting cancer</b>. <br>The author manages to highlight these issues and manifest wholesome emotions without making you think "oh god not a sob story" - instead you're really hoping that these kids make it. Achieve their goals - become a success. You're invested in their happiness. <br><br>I also like that fact that Kit, despite what her parents put her though - loves her parents - that shows she's a genuinely kind and loving person - she NEVER comes across as a brat. No entitlement POOR-ME stuff here. <br><br>Life can throw many challenges - and reading this book - it really was uplifting to see how protective and strong 5 boys can be for each-other. And the manner in which their brotherly love was conveyed was beautiful - the nuances skilfully woven into the story to manifest love without melodrama. <br>Witnessing the family interactions and Kit's burgeoning relationship with them was profoundly gratifying.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427588778ra/14290640.gif" width="600" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>=============<br><b>
  <u>Plot</u>
</b><br><br>Kit is a runaway (in NYC) where she encounters Logan at his family run Tattoo parlour. She's hoping to have a tat and brings with her a drawing that she designed. He gets frisky with her and she punches him in the nose (she's learnt to be tough) and storms out leaving behind that design by accident. Logan is intrigued by the design (he's an artist) and pursues her. It's as they become acquainted that the story develops. Logan being deaf and Kit being unable to read properly makes communicating extremely difficult. The challenges they face (poverty, secrets, building trust, etc) all come into play in a riveting story that manifests the struggles, sacrifices and love a family endures. <br><br><b>
  <u>The Characters</u>
</b><br><br><b>Logan</b>: is an endearing 21 yo, <i>who happens to be deaf</i>. <br>He's intelligent, artistic, funny and kind. Additionally, he's had to make huge sacrifices for his family (just as they have had to make sacrifices for him). He's the middle brother (2 older and 2 younger). <br>After his mother's death, plus due to his disability (and other hardships) <i>he finds it difficult to become close to people</i>, <u>particularly women</u>. <br><u>Generally I loath playboy</u> characters (<i>snore</i>), BUT as we get to understand Logan and his background, we can see the depth he possess and admire him for his resilience. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427079391ra/14173552.gif" width="600" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Kit</b>: (<i>not her real name</i>) is a 19 yo, guitar-playing runaway <i>who happens to be dyslexic</i>. <br>She's had to put up with many ignorant people not understanding her disability and assuming she's stupid. <br>She doesn't want pity and she's struggling to become independent. She's not the spoiled, self-absorbed teenage angst-y melodramatic type but a tough cookie who works hard. She really cares for Logan and his brothers and it's enjoyable reading their interactions.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427589040i/14290696.jpg" width="600" height="600" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </span>
  <a data-text-id="5001540456296282998" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_796762726" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/796762726" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/796762726?book_show_action=true">Dec 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=aestas-made-me-read-it">aestas-made-me-read-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series-book-1">series-book-1</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series-faves-book-1">series-faves-book-1</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer796762726" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5533930469551322668"><b>4.5 sweet and heartfelt stars</b><br/><br/>I randomly plucked this book from my kindle, and it took me completely by surprise! Entertaining and meaningful right from the start, I was instantly addicted and I absolutely loved it!<br/><br/>Logan is a sexy, pierced and heavily tatted tattoo artist. He is also deaf, but lost his hearing at the age of 13 so he knows how to speak, he just chooses not to and hasn’t spoken a word for eight years. He meets Kit when she comes to him for a tattoo, and the cocky manwhore is immedi</span>
  <span id="freeText5533930469551322668" style="display:none"><b>4.5 sweet and heartfelt stars</b><br /><br />I randomly plucked this book from my kindle, and it took me completely by surprise! Entertaining and meaningful right from the start, I was instantly addicted and I absolutely loved it!<br /><br />Logan is a sexy, pierced and heavily tatted tattoo artist. He is also deaf, but lost his hearing at the age of 13 so he knows how to speak, he just chooses not to and hasn’t spoken a word for eight years. He meets Kit when she comes to him for a tattoo, and the cocky manwhore is immediately attracted to the mysterious, guarded, and utterly beautiful girl. But when he acts like his usual, manwhoring self she is unimpressed, in fact is highly offended, and punches him in the face before leaving. You’ve gotta love her for that! It’s the beginning of a beautiful relationship!<br /><br />Kit is homeless. She survives by busking in the subways during the day, and sleeping in homeless shelters at night. When she and Logan unintentionally meet again, he is determined to get to know her and now that he’s behaving like the sweetheart he is, things go way more smoothly. Kit has a learning disability and doesn’t read well, but Logan is so enamoured with her, he wants to be able to communicate with her, so he does what he hasn’t done in eight years. He talks to her. But only to her. <br /><br />When Logan realises that she is all alone with nowhere to go he offers her a place to stay for the night in the home he shares with his four brothers. From there, a tentative friendship develops between the two of them, which quickly grows into something more as they start to fall for each other. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I think I’m in like.”</i>
</blockquote><br />I love this relationship! There is chemistry, it’s believable and it’s incredibly special. What Logan and Kit find together is so meaningful to the both of them – they accept each other without question, and their openness and honesty about what they are feeling is gorgeous. The two of them together absolutely melted me. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I’ve been locked in my own world for a really long time … And I felt like maybe, just maybe, we were locked in our own little worlds and could let each other out.”</i>
</blockquote><br />Kit’s story is heartbreaking. She is incredibly guarded, and hides a big secret. She so desperately wants Logan, but is terrified of hurting him so she keeps herself closed off and doesn’t share her past. Instead she keeps a part of herself from him, but gives him what she can, and hopes that it will be enough. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i> “She’s going to break your fucking heart, man.” … <br />I know. She’s going to break my fucking heart. Because I’ve never wanted anything with anyone the way I want something I can’t even define with her.</i>
</blockquote><br />And OMG, I am madly in love with Logan. He’s an absolute sweetheart, and the way that he cares for Kit is beautiful! Having never been in love before, he is knocked on his ass by Kit, and his devotion to her and confidence that they belong together is gorgeous. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I want you to trust me. And you don’t. Not yet. But you might one day.”<br /><br /> “If I ever get to fucking be inside you, I want to know what to call you. I want to at least know your name. Because when that happens, you’re going to fucking own me.” I tip her face up so she’s looking at me. “Do you understand?”<br />She looks unsure.<br />“You’re going to own me … And there’s nothing I want more.”</i>
</blockquote><br />And just to add to the awesome, Kit is very quickly accepted into Logan’s family by his boisterous and gorgeous brothers, and the relationship that she develops with them is absolutely beautiful! I love the Reed boys. They rib and tease, but they are fiercely protective of each other and the love that they have for each other is obvious in all that they do. And the way they include Kit into their family is magic. I want to be adopted by them!<br /><br />But when the unthinkable happens, Emily is faced with a heartbreaking decision that could destroy the happiness that she has found. But is it worth the cost?<br /><br />I wasn't too sure what to expect when I picked this one up, but it turned out to be one of those reads that I instantly loved, and I LOVE when that happens! Told in dual POV, it’s a quick read that moves at a great pace with lots of heart, some laughs, sweet moments and a beautiful romance with a nice amount of sexy time. There were a couple of inconsistencies, but they didn’t bother me too much. And that big dramatic ending (not a cliffy exactly, but not somewhere I was expecting the book to finish) had my heart in my throat, and me reaching straight for the next book of the series.<br /><br />I loved it – 4.5 stars.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5533930469551322668" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_680278667" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/680278667" />
    <a title="Jess-i-ca ~Sometimes a Gif Witch~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8740772-jess-i-ca-sometimes-a-gif-witch"><img alt="Jess-i-ca ~Sometimes a Gif Witch~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487382075p2/8740772.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer704160039" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6969904457832056849">I'd have to agree with a lot of other reviewers when I say that even though I knew about the deaf hero, I got way more than I expected from this book. He wasn't just a deaf guy. He really is a hero. An every day kind of hero. He saves the girl. And he's deaf. <br/><br/>But the ending...srsly? SRSLY?!?! See how I shortened that word? People do that all the time, right? So do authors lately. This book was half a story. A very good half a story. I will absolutely be reading the next one, but I can't give a f</span>
  <span id="freeText6969904457832056849" style="display:none">I'd have to agree with a lot of other reviewers when I say that even though I knew about the deaf hero, I got way more than I expected from this book. He wasn't just a deaf guy. He really is a hero. An every day kind of hero. He saves the girl. And he's deaf. <br /><br />But the ending...srsly? SRSLY?!?! See how I shortened that word? People do that all the time, right? So do authors lately. This book was half a story. A very good half a story. I will absolutely be reading the next one, but I can't give a five star review to half a story. Maybe when I finish it. As it was, this is more than worth the time, and since I got it as a freebie months ago, I feel like a lucky girl. I'm officially in LOVE with the Reed brothers. There is a depth to them that you rarely find in contemporary romance. These are not all the big, strong, strapping brothers...most of whom are in law enforcement, or are ex Navy SEALS, or something to that effect. These guys are normal, wonderful, loving brothers who have had a hell of a life and have come out on this side of a crap-tastic beginning to become really fantastic <b>men.</b> </span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=audible">audible</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=series">series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1130476756" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17131484076658191483"><b>I liked this one! The characters were lovable, it’s fast-paced, sweet, and sexy. It caught my attention from the very beginning and had me smiling like crazy.</b><br/><br/>Logan is a tattoo artist who works with his brothers at the shop they own and he is also deaf. He’s pretty much a manwhore, never sleeping with the same girl twice and never forming any kind of friendship/attachment. He meets Kit when she comes in to get a tattoo and tries to treat her like any other girl, getting pretty handsy with her aft</span>
  <span id="freeText17131484076658191483" style="display:none"><b>I liked this one! The characters were lovable, it’s fast-paced, sweet, and sexy. It caught my attention from the very beginning and had me smiling like crazy.</b><br /><br />Logan is a tattoo artist who works with his brothers at the shop they own and he is also deaf. He’s pretty much a manwhore, never sleeping with the same girl twice and never forming any kind of friendship/attachment. He meets Kit when she comes in to get a tattoo and tries to treat her like any other girl, getting pretty handsy with her after only a couple minutes. Kit definitely isn’t having it and ends up punching him in the face and rushing away. I really loved how this began, showing how strong and feisty Kit can be and it totally made me laugh. <br /><br />Kit is a performer, busking in the subways and on the streets for tips. She ran away from her family and is now homeless, just trying to make it day to day. When Logan runs into her on the street he ends up taking her out to apologize. Once he realizes she homeless, he insists on bringing her home with him. Logan lives with his four brothers. The dynamic between the five of them is pretty awesome to see. They joke and tease but are incredibly loyal and loving as well. <br /><br />Things between Logan and Kit move really quickly. Their feelings come on fast and strong. It did feel a bit insta-lovey to me, but because this is kind of a short book in general it was okay. It also helped that Logan was very adamant about knowing more about Kit and who she really is. He wanted her trust and to know her secrets before their relationship could progress to something physical. <br /><i>
  <blockquote>“But even more than I want to lick you all over and make you cry out my name and swear you see God, I want you to trust me. And you don’t. Not yet. But you might one day.”<br />…<br />I wanted to reach over and touch him, but he doesn’t want that from me. He wants all of me. And I’m not free to give it all away. I’ll never be free.</blockquote>
</i><br />I liked the set up for this book. Kit’s situation and how all the boys embrace her was so sweet, it really felt like she fit into their family perfectly. I also loved her unique connection with Matt and the other brothers, it made it feel even more special. Logan being deaf was another interesting aspect and how he opened up and shared a part of himself with Kit that he hasn’t since he became deaf at thirteen. Their romance and connection was really heartwarming. <br /><i>
  <blockquote>“I’ve been locked in my own world for a really long time,” he says. “I have an excuse to keep people away, because of my disability. And then I saw your tattoo…” I turn his wrist over and trace my finger across it. He shudders at my touch, closing his eyes tightly. “And I felt like maybe, just maybe, we were each locked in our own little worlds and could let each other out.”</blockquote>
</i><br />I ended up enjoying this one! It was really light on the angst and it didn’t feel like there was any unnecessary drama. Maybe some things were a bit coincidental/predictable and the instalove thing was there, but it was fast and a sweet read overall. I had no idea that Logan and Kit’s story was more than one book. Toward the end, with so much unresolved I was worried how it would all be wrapped up so I’m glad they have another book. I’m really excited to continue on with this series! <br /><br /><b>
  <u>Audio comments:</u>
</b> <br /><i>I really wasn’t a big fan of the narrator for this story. Dara Rosenberg sounds young so she did feel right for Kit, being that she’s nineteen. But when it came time to do the voices for the men, she sounded really whiney and annoying to me. She made them sound kind of immature/jokey even when it didn’t call for it at that moment. It was really distracting at first and I considered stopping. I ended up continuing and despite her horrible male narration, I did end up falling in love with Logan and his brothers. If I had read this story I think it would be a solid 4 star no problem, but I’m having a hard time separating my feelings for the story and how the narration may have affected my connection.</i><br /><br /><b>3.5 stars</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="17131484076658191483" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_880240419" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/880240419" />
    <a title="Plamena" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14813237-plamena"><img alt="Plamena" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1405071408p2/14813237.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/880240419?book_show_action=true">Mar 13, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Plamena" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Plamena" href="/user/show/14813237-plamena">Plamena</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer880240419" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer945759022223085954"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br/> <br/><i>
  <b>“I’d talk to this girl all day long if it means she’ll smile at me like that.”</b>
</i><br/><br/>I have to admit this book surprised me. It is such a sweet story! I couldn’t put it down. It is well written and it will melt your heart!<br/><br/>Sooo..the story: <br/> <br/>Logan Reed is a seriously hot tattoo artist. He is also deaf and doesn’t speak. Not that he can’t...he just didn’t want to...until now. When a beautiful girl asks him for a tattoo, Logan is in a trance for few minutes. She is gorgeous. And when he tries</span>
  <span id="freeText945759022223085954" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br> <br><i>
  <b>“I’d talk to this girl all day long if it means she’ll smile at me like that.”</b>
</i><br><br>I have to admit this book surprised me. It is such a sweet story! I couldn’t put it down. It is well written and it will melt your heart!<br><br>Sooo..the story: <br> <br>Logan Reed is a seriously hot tattoo artist. He is also deaf and doesn’t speak. Not that he can’t...he just didn’t want to...until now. When a beautiful girl asks him for a tattoo, Logan is in a trance for few minutes. She is gorgeous. And when he tries to flirt with her- she breaks his nose and leaves! LOL<br><br>Kit can’t stop thinking about the jerk that tried to touch her in a seriously inappropriate way. She just wanted a tattoo. But she has bigger problems- like what is she going to eat tonight and where is she going to sleep!? When the sexy tattoo artist finds her and offers her dinner and a bed to sleep....she doesn’t want to accept. But he literally carries her to his place. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396859545i/9195887._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Logan is a total men whore. He doesn’t want commitment and has never slept with a girl twice. But Kit is different. She is beautiful, intriguing and fun. But she doesn’t want to tell him anything about herself. She has too many secrets. He needs to find a way to make her trust him but it won’t be easy (if possible at all). <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396859545i/9195888.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What I loved about this story is that Logan is not disabled. I didn’t feel sorry for him and the fact that he is deaf didn’t make me sad. He is confident and playful...absolutely charming. But his best feature is his heart!!! <br><br><i>
  <b>"I want to take you to bed, and make love to you all night long." He cocks a grin at me. "Lips. Tongue. Fingers. Teeth."</b>
</i><br><br>Logan lives with his four brothers and they all are also seriously fun. One of them is really sick and is fighting cancer...That was a sad moment in the book. But there is always hope. <br><br>I didn’t know there was another book about Logan and Kit. I hope it is as good as this one. I am starting it immediately. <br></span>

<div id="review_682016532" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/682016532?book_show_action=true">Jul 31, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="HJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="HJ" href="/user/show/7698316-hj">HJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7698316-hj?shelf=new-adult-young-adult">new-adult-young-adult</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer682016532" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17957040456685945760">No one is more surprised than me that I really liked this NA book. <br/><br/>Great things - <br/><br/>1st person POV - Both sides. Likable characters - all the way around. <br/><br/>Realistic angst - not the 'rape' or murdered/suicide background that we see so often. <br/><br/>The characters didn't go into 'heat' every time they saw each other - Thank you, thank you, thank you!!! Let me point out that the ebook contains 2 versions - Sexy and Sweet. I read the sexy version, which had just the right level of sexual activity (for me). Le</span>
  <span id="freeText17957040456685945760" style="display:none">No one is more surprised than me that I really liked this NA book. <br /><br />Great things - <br /><br />1st person POV - Both sides. Likable characters - all the way around. <br /><br />Realistic angst - not the 'rape' or murdered/suicide background that we see so often. <br /><br />The characters didn't go into 'heat' every time they saw each other - Thank you, thank you, thank you!!! Let me point out that the ebook contains 2 versions - Sexy and Sweet. I read the sexy version, which had just the right level of sexual activity (for me). Let me also point out that this means that the book is done at the 50% mark. But it's not a super short book, though. <br /><br />What could have made it a bit MORE realistic - more details on the illness of one of the secondary characters. It wasn't the main plot of the book, but it was important enough that it stood out to me that I couldn't 'picture' what exactly the illness was.<br /><br />Still, for those getting tired of the same old NA books out there, this was a refreshing change.<br /><br />Recommended.<br /><br />:) <br /> </span>

		    <b>
          <a title="YA Buddy Readers&#39; Corner ♥" class="actionLink" href="https://www.goodreads.com/topic/show/1495034-tall-tatted-and-tempting-by-tammy-falkner---restarting-october-11th-201">YA Buddy Readers&#39;...:</a>
        </b>
      
			<a class="actionLink" href="/topic/show/1495034-tall-tatted-and-tempting-by-tammy-falkner---restarting-october-11th-201">Tall, Tatted and Tempting by Tammy Falkner - Restarting October 11th 2019</a>
		</td>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('iYLP/dBnGEyaRV+Ft4QFkq8qBLRyuUG2v4yo6vZg582Akxn9ekQBg4M5Ccrln5YYmvSzLRP5EB6RnhOQSsnYSg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('lbjkcRL5mzpxHFgQeZf0tFANpfZu9HvjAyoadB2lORycqTJxuNqC9WhgDl8rjGc+ZdMSbw+0KkstOKEOoQwGmw==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer7977316375124069218">Tammy Falkner lives on a farm in a lovely, sprawling little town in rural NC with her beekeeper husband and a house full of boys, a few dogs, and a cat or two (or five – who has time to count?).   <span id="freeText7977316375124069218" style="display:none">Tammy Falkner lives on a farm in a lovely, sprawling little town in rural NC with her beekeeper husband and a house full of boys, a few dogs, and a cat or two (or five – who has time to count?). As half of the Lydia Dare team, she has co-written ten books, including the Westfield Wolves series and the Gentlemen Vampyre series. A huge fan of Regency England, she often wonders what other kinds of magical, mythical and strange creatures might live and interact within the ton. Exploring the theory that the fae can walk between Regency England and their own land, Tammy spends as much time as possible with the lords and ladies of society, horse-drawn carriages, and elegant balls. Now add to that some faeries, a little murder, a bit of mayhem, and a troublesome garden gnome, and you have her exciting new series. She hopes you enjoys her world as much as she does.<br /><br />Also writes as<br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/3112090.Lydia_Dare" rel="nofollow noopener">Lydia Dare</a></span>
